Sketch & Design: From Foundations to Creativity
An International Guide to Artistic Expression through Lines

โ๏ธ ููุฏูู ูุณุฎู ุงูฺฏูุณ 

Sketch & Design: From Foundations to Creativity
(For international publication, NFT, and Amazon)

๐ Introduction

Sketching is more than drawing. It is a silent language of lines, a dynamic method of thinking, and a timeless act of creation. From the earliest cave markings to the complex digital forms of modern design, sketching has always been the foundation upon which great ideas are born, tested, and transformed.

This bookโSketch & Designโis not merely a tutorial. It is a guided journey through the world of visual expression, designed for artists, architects, designers, and thinkers at all levels.

Across three progressive sectionsโFoundations, Advanced Techniques, and Creative Explorationsโthis book offers a carefully structured approach to building skills, developing insight, and ultimately liberating the imagination.

Here, you will not only learn how to draw a chair, a tree, or a handโbut how to see. How to observe deeply. How to find movement in stillness and form in emptiness.
Each stroke is a decision. Each page is a dialogue between mind and material.

Whether you are a beginner picking up a pencil for the first time or a professional seeking new artistic challenges, this book invites you to rediscover the joy of pure creationโone line at a time.

โ Jamshid Smaily
